<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Interim Management Report<a name="InterimManagementReport_214246"></a></font></b></h1>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. Business Activity</font></b><a name="a1_BusinessActivity_214249"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
(&#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148; or &#147;the Company&#148;) is a leading provider of deposition
equipment to the semiconductor industry. The Company&#146;s technology solutions are
used by a diverse range of customers worldwide to build advanced components for
electronic and opto-electronic applications based on compound, silicon, or
organic semiconductor materials. Such components are used in displays, signaling,
lighting, fiber optic communication systems, wireless and mobile telephony
applications, optical and electronic storage devices, computing, as well as a
range of other leading-edge technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company markets and sells its products worldwide, principally through its
direct sales organization and appointed dealers and sales representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
business activities include developing, producing and installing equipment for
coating semiconductor materials, process engineering, consulting and training,
including ongoing customer support.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
supplies to customers both full production-scale chemical vapor deposition
systems and small scale systems for Research and Development use and
small-scale production use.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
product range includes customized production and research scale compound
semiconductor systems capable of depositing material films on up to 95 x
two-inch diameter wafers per single production run, or smaller multiples of 4
to 6 inch diameter wafers, employing Metal-Organic Chemical Vapor Deposition (&#147;MOCVD&#148;)
or organic thin film deposition on up to Gen. 3.5 substrates, including Polymer
Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;PVPD&#148;) or Organic Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148;) for Organic
Light Emitting Diodes (&#147;OLED&#148;) applications or Plasma Enhanced Chemical Vapor
Phase Deposition (&#147;PECVD&#148;) for depositing complex Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon
Nanotubes or Nanowires). AIXTRON also manufactures full production and research
scale deposition systems for silicon semiconductor market applications capable
of depositing material films on wafers of up to 300 mm diameter, employing
technologies such as: Chemical Vapor Deposition (&#147;CVD&#148;), Atomic Vapor
Deposition (&#147;AVD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148;) and Atomic Layer Deposition (&#147;ALD&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\brama\09-32226-1\task3770397\32226-1-be.htm',USER='105435',CD='Oct 28 20:52 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. Important Factors of the
Reporting Period</font></b><a name="a2_ImportantFactorsOfTheReporting_214257"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TV
backlighting continues to drive order intake: new all time high</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Equipment order intake in
Q3/2009 reached EUR 117.6m, and consequently was 103% higher than in Q2 and
125% higher year-on-year. As the demand for LED applications, and TV
backlighting in particular, bring the AIXTRON order volume to a new all time
high, market sentiment and faster than predicted adoption suggest that this
trend will continue into 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Benefitting from the
increasing business volume, Q3/2009 gross margin, EBIT margin, and net profit
margin (42%, 20%, and 14% respectively) rose sequentially and on a year-on-year
comparison basis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Strategies
Unlimited increases market estimates again</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Within its latest
August&nbsp;2009 report, Strategies Unlimited (an independent semiconductor
market research institute) again increased its High Brightness (&#147;HB&#148;) LED
growth estimates for the period until the year 2013, especially for</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
applications such as LED backlighting and general illumination. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the beginning
of the year, in February, the institute had published lower figures for this
same period, influenced by the market mood at that time arising from the
financial and economic crisis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However,
aided by the increased applications and substantial competitive capacity
increase, the cost of LEDs is predicted to continue to drop while their
performance continues to improve.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under
these conditions, the market for HB LEDs in illumination is, according to
Strategies Unlimited, now forecast to reach nearly USD 2.85bn by 2013,
corresponding to a CAGR (2008 through 2013) of 40%. This market development is
earlier than previously predicted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Other
applications with the potential for a larger than recently published market
growth over the next five years, include backlighting of notebook computer
displays, LCD TVs, and monitors. By 2013, the market for HB LEDs in signs and
displays is estimated by Strategies Unlimited to reach USD 7.2bn, which corresponds
to a CAGR of 55%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">US-Dollar
drifting lower against the Euro</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After the period of strength
for the US-Dollar against the Euro seen at the beginning of the year, the
US-currency drifted lower against the Euro starting in March, eventually
breaching the USD 1.40 level by end of May.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The weakening US-Dollar-trend
continued in Q3/2009. A period of strengthening stock market data and positive
economic news was coincidental with the falling value of the dollar taking it
to a year-low against the Euro at USD 1.48 by September&nbsp;22nd. At
quarter-end, the Euro bought 1.46 USD.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nevertheless, the average
US-Dollar/Euro exchange rate of Q3/2009 was USD 1.42, 6% stronger than the USD
1.50 average of Q3/2008. This has in turn positively influenced AIXTRON&#146;s
Q3/2009 comparable revenues, gross margin and EBIT, as more than 70% of AIXTRON
revenues are generally transacted in US-Dollars, with only roughly 20% of the
Company&#146;s cost being in US-Dollars.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The UK-Pound also began to
suffer against other currencies during the period, notably the US-Dollar and
the Euro, driven by the market expectation of an extended period of low
interest rates in the UK.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON routinely employs a
variety of hedging instruments to mitigate the effects of currency movements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Market
capitalization exceeds EUR 1 billion mark</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In mid July 2009,
the AIXTRON market capitalization rose above the EUR 1 billion mark. With
91,357,552 ordinary non-par value AIXTRON-shares outstanding at that time
(consisting of 90.894.616 shares already registered with the commercial
register and additional 462.936 issued under stock option programs but not yet
registered with the commercial register), at a share price of EUR 10.95, the
AIXTRON market capitalization became just over EUR 1 billion for the first time
since June 2002.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On August&nbsp;25,
the AIXTRON-share was added to the components of the Dow Jones STOXX</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;600 Index with a 0.0304% weighting. The 600
index stocks are ranked by free float market capitalization and represent
large, mid and small capitalization companies across 18 countries of the
European region.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">By mid
September&nbsp;2009, the AIXTRON market capitalization rose further to exceed
EUR 1.5 billion. At quarter-end, on September&nbsp;30, 2009, the market
capitalization had reached EUR 1.7bn </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .35in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">with a closing share price of EUR 18.62.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .35in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
considerable increase in market capitalization was coincidental with an
increasing number of large institutional AIXTRON investors. A minimum market
capitalisation value is often set as a minimum threshold for large
institutional investors to consider an investment. This AIXTRON shareholder mix
change is seen by Management a positive development in the company&#146;s
shareholder base.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .35in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fidelity
becomes largest single shareholder group</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September&nbsp;3,
2009, Fidelity Management&nbsp;&amp; Research Company, Boston, MA, USA,
informed the Company according to Article&nbsp;21, Section&nbsp;1 of the WpHG,
that via shares its voting rights on AIXTRON AG had exceeded the 10% limit on August&nbsp;26,
2009. On that day, the Fidelity group, through subsidiary investments, held
10.14% (this corresponds to </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9,264,482 vo</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ting rights) of the
AIXTRON share capital.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
US-headquartered Fidelity group is one of the biggest investment companies in
the world and provides a large family of mutual funds all over the globe.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Final
Acceptance of first 300mm Cluster Tool by Philipps-University of Marburg</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The final acceptance
documentation for the newly developed AIXTRON CRIUS</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;CCS</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;MOVPE system with 300mm wafer configuration,
delivered in Q1/2009 and then successfully installed and commissioned, has been
signed off by Philipps-University of Marburg at the end of Q3/2009.
Consequently, the total revenue of this previously unproven technology was
recorded within Q3/2009 as silicon revenue.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The cluster tool includes two
silicon- and III/V-based material modules and is therefore suitable for the
growth of III/V semiconductor structures on commercially available silicon
wafers, with the aim of monolithically integrating optoelectronics with silicon-based
microelectronics.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The successful system
acceptance provides further evidence for the emerging convergence of
conventional silicon technology with compound semiconductor technology. In
Management&#146;s opinion, AIXTRON&#146;s market leading core competence with compound
material technology can also be effectively employed as a complex solution
technology for silicon customers. Potential future applications are perceived
to be in next-generation data communication devices and highly efficient
silicon solar cells.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">New
Research Project: Semiconductor-Nanowires for Solar Cells and LEDs (NaSoL)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During Q3/2009, the NaSoL
research project, supported by the state of Northrhine-Westfalia (in the scope
of their technology and innovation program TIP) was formally approved and
started.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the project leadership
of AIXTRON, and in cooperation with the University of Duisburg-Essen and other
industrial partners, the research project team will design and build a
technology platform for LEDs and solar cells employing nanowire-structures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The project&#146;s goal is to
develop new growth processes for nanowires, replacing traditional semiconductor
layers, using metal organic gasphase epitaxy. The plan is to increase the
efficiency both of solar cells and of white LEDs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Award for
AIXTRON founder Dr.&nbsp;J&#252;rgensen during Semicon Europa</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In Q3/2009, AIXTRON was
informed that its founder and current Deputy Chairman of the AIXTRON
Supervisory Board Dr.&nbsp;Holger J&#252;rgensen had been selected as winner of the
European SEMI Award 2009. The award was presented to him during Semicon Europa
2009, in Dresden, Germany on October&nbsp;6.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 1983, Dr.&nbsp;J&#252;rgensen,
together with two colleagues had originally founded AIXTRON, with the initial
objective of developing and, ultimately, commercializing, MOCVD deposition
technology. With his engineering vision and commercial drive he has played a major
role in bringing MOCVD deposition equipment from the very early days of small
R&amp;D systems to today&#146;s mass production scale equipment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Dr.&nbsp;J&#252;rgensen has not
only played a pivotal role in the creation of the MOCVD industry, but he also
laid the essential technical foundations for AIXTRON&#146;s subsequent
diversification into adjacent technologies, including OLED and Carbon Nanotube
material deposition and provided a clear roadmap path to the impending
convergence of Compound and Silicon technologies.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">3. Results of Operations</font></b><a name="a3_ResultsOfOperations_221627"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1. Development
of Revenues</font></b><a name="a3_1_DevelopmentOfRevenues_221630"></a></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the first nine months of 2009, AIXTRON recorded revenues of EUR&nbsp;184.9m, a
EUR&nbsp;7.2m or 4% reduction compared to EUR&nbsp;192.1m in the same nine
months period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
positive average US-Dollar/Euro rate (9M/2009: USD1.36 versus 9M/2008 USD1.52;
+12%), and the progressively strong revenue volumes within the first nine
months of the year, contributed to the near attainment of last year&#146;s strong
revenue number.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
EUR -7.2m difference in revenues year-on-year was largely driven by lower
service and spare parts revenues (EUR -3.5m), primarily due to the
under-utilization of customers&#146; equipment in the beginning of the year. This
market condition was strongly influenced by customer&#146;s inventory reduction
programs brought about by fears of recession at that time. Consequently,
service and spare parts revenues only generated 9% of total 9M/2009 revenues
(9M/2008: 11%).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nine
monthly sales of compound semiconductor deposition equipment (of EUR 158.2m)
were 2% less in comparison to the same period last year. This strong
comparative performance in 2009 was largely possible, despite the recession,
because of the significant Q2 and Q3 quarterly revenue volumes, which
predominantly stem from customers&#146; increased purchasing of systems for the
production of LEDs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
proportion of revenues from silicon semiconductor deposition equipment to total
revenues remained the same at 5%. Included in the nine-monthly figure of 2009
(EUR 9.3m) is the total revenue (EUR 4.1m) of a newly developed 300m cluster
tool for Philipps-University of Marburg.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">21.0</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-3.6</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-17</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">80%
of total revenues in 9M/2009 were delivered to customers in Asia. The
comparatively high European revenue share (15% in 9M/2009 versus 6% in 9M/2008)
was significantly influenced by the Plastic Logic system revenue recorded in
Q1/2009. The remaining revenue, with an almost unchanged 5% share, was
generated in the USA.</font></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.2</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">20</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>

 <tr>
  <td width="38%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:38.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 20.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net other operating (income) and expenses</font></p>

  </td>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.1</font></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.5%;">

</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cost of
sales</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> improved from 60% of revenues in 9M/2008 to 57% of revenues in the
current reporting period. In absolute terms, cost of sales reduced by 8% from
EUR&nbsp;114.8m in 9M/2008 to EUR&nbsp;105.7m in 9M/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At
the same time, the <b>gross margin</b>
improved by 3 percentage points from 40% of revenues to 43% of revenues, while
the <b>gross profit</b> increased in absolute
terms by 2% to EUR&nbsp;79.2m in 9M/2009 (9M/2008: EUR&nbsp;77.3m). This
improvement resulted from a more favorable revenue mix with a higher percentage
of final acceptances especially in the first quarter of 2009 and a favorable
USD/EUR exchange rate.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared
to the first nine months of 2008, <b>operating costs</b>
in 9M/2009 decreased by 4% to EUR 50.2m in absolute terms. Operating costs
relative to revenues remained stable at 27%, and were influenced by the
following factors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Selling
expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> relative to revenues, improved to only 9% of revenues
in the first nine months of 2009 (9M/2008: 11%). In absolute terms, the <b>selling expenses</b> were substantially lower (by 20%) at
EUR&nbsp;16.3m year-on-year (9M/2008: EUR 20.5m). This improvement in relative
and absolute terms was mainly due to a different geographical mix of sales and
therefore lower variable sales commissions, and controlled discretionary
expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">General
and administration expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased to EUR 16.1m or 9%
of revenues in 9M/2009 (9M/2008: EUR&nbsp;14.2m or 7% of revenues) principally
due to provisions for profit-related variable administration expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared
to the same period last year,<b> Research and development </b>spending
increased by EUR 4.2m or 20% in 9M/2009 to EUR 24.9m (9M/2008: EUR 20.7m), the
largest single element being the expense for one publicly funded R&amp;D
project of EUR 1.6m in Q1/2009. Relative to revenues, R&amp;D spending
increased by 2 percentage points from 11% to 13%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
continued focus on </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">R&amp;D across the Group is
driven by Management&#146;s determination to remain a major player in markets judged
by many to hold significant growth opportunities for many years to come.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net other
operating income and expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> more than doubled by EUR
3.9m, resulting in an operating income of EUR&nbsp;7.1m in the first nine
months of 2009 (9M/2008: EUR&nbsp;3.2m of income).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included
in the other operating income of 9M/2009 are the gains made from the sale of
the Aachen office building (EUR 1.3m) and </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a compensation
payment for a single cancelled order (EUR 2.5m), both booked in Q1/2009. Also </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">accounted for in
the 9M/2009 other operating income are higher R&amp;D grants of EUR 0.8m. A
decrease of bad debt provisions by EUR 1.3m also positively influenced the net </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">other
operating income and expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Negative
foreign exchange effects, arising principally from USD/EUR currency
transactions and translations and from hedging contract premiums, resulted in a
net expense of EUR 1.4m in 9M/2009 versus a net income of EUR 1.3m in the
previous year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating
income (EBIT)</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> in 9M/2009 was EUR&nbsp;29.0m with a 16% margin, 16%
and 3 percentage points higher year-on-year (9M/2008: EUR 25.0m; 13% margin),
principally due to a good revenue mix, a still favorable USD/EUR exchange rate,
and higher other operating income items.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Result
before taxes</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased by 7%, from EUR 27.6m in 9M/2008 to EUR
29.6m in 9M/2009, despite lower interest income,.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
recorded a <b>tax expense</b> of EUR 9.2m of the
profit before tax in the first nine months of 2009, with an effective tax rate
of 31%*, similar to 9M/2008 (EUR 8.7m or 32% of the profit before taxes).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
9M/2009 <b>net income</b> was EUR 20.4m, 8% up
year-on-year from EUR 18.9m in 9M/2008.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*
(based on the expected tax rate for the full financial year 2009)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">151.0</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">96</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-1.9</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-1</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s total nine months 2009 <b>equipment
order intake</b> was 2% lower than last year&#146;s high level of EUR 210.2m,
coming in at EUR 206.7m.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nevertheless, the 9M/2009 order volume reflects a
progressively rising order trend, whereas in 2008, the nine month total was
reached on a sequentially declining quarterly order intake trend. The Q3/2009
order intake figure (EUR 117.6m; an increase of 103% sequentially, and 125%
year-on-year) represents the highest quarterly order volume in AIXTRON&#146;s
history.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 206.1m or 99.7% of the total value of 9M/2009
equipment orders (EUR 198.4m or 94.4% of total order intake in 9M/2008) came
from </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">compound semiconductor equipment</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
customers, who are predominantly focused on the production of high brightness
LEDs and the corresponding end-market applications. Consequently, the absolute </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">order intake for
compound semiconductor equipment</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
increased </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">by 4% in a year-on-year nine-monthly comparison.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This positive development for compound semiconductor
equipment marks the beginning of a new LED investment cycle, which started
after the low point of demand in Q1/2009, and is primarily driven by the
increased adoption of LED TV applications. The previous LED investment cycle
with its equipment demand peak in Q4/2007 had been primarily driven by notebook
backlighting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
proportion of orders received in the first nine months of 2009 for silicon
semiconductor equipment dropped to 0.3% of total equipment order intake, from
5.6% in 9M/2008. In absolute numbers, the order intake for silicon
semiconductor equipment decreased to EUR 0.6m in 9M/2009 from EUR 11.8m in
9M/2008, due to the persistently negative memory market environment. Management
believes that there is little evidence to suggest that this situation will
improve during the last quarter of this year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Separately;
the development work being conducted on next-generation memory and logic
equipment continues, with customer demonstrations and film development work
being done within the Company&#146;s research labs and at customers&#146; facilities.
This work, combined with the involvement of Sunnyvale staff in next generation
compound and other group nano-technology projects, means that the team in
Sunnyvale continue to make a positive and valuable contribution to the Group&#146;s
objectives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b>equipment order backlog</b>
of EUR 152.4m at September&nbsp;30, 2009 is 4% lower than at the same point in
time in 2008 (EUR 158.1m). However, with the increasing 2009 order intake
volumes, the September&nbsp;30 order backlog has further increased (by 39%)
versus the June&nbsp;30 figure of EUR109.4m. The Management expects that about
EUR 88m of the 9M/2009 period end backlog will be converted into revenues
before the end of the year 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The order backlog for compound semiconductor equipment
was EUR 149.1m as of September&nbsp;30, 2009 (98% of total backlog), representing
a 1% decrease year-on-year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The remaining backlog figure of EUR </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.3m (2% of total
backlog) is made up of silicon semiconductor equipment orders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
a matter of internal policy, AIXTRON records only equipment orders as actual
order intake and order backlog, if the Company has received a firm purchase
order, an agreed deposit and a customer-confirmed delivery date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Financial Position</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;"> and Net Assets</font><a name="a4_FinancialPositionAndNetAssets_221700"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company recorded no <b>bank borrowings</b> as of September&nbsp;30,
2009 and December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
<b>equity ratio</b> decreased to 65% as of September&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2009,
from 68% as of December&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2008, principally due to a higher balance
sheet total because of the increasing business volume (higher cash and cash
deposits on the asset side; more advanced payments, trade payables and tax
liabilities on the liabilities side).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The AIXTRON Group&#146;s <b>capital
expenditures</b> of the first nine months of 2009 amounted to EUR 6.8m,
the large majority of which was related to purchases of technical equipment
(including testing and laboratory equipment). In 2008, the nine months capital
expenditures were 36% higher (at EUR 9.2m) because of investments at that time
into the new headquarters in Herzogenrath.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>property, plant and equipment</b> decreased to
EUR&nbsp;32.8m as per September&nbsp;30,
2009 (</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 39.3m as of December&nbsp;31,
2008), principally due to the sale of the Aachen office building.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The slight decrease in recorded <b>goodwill </b>from
</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 58.7m as per December&nbsp;31, 2008 t</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o
EUR</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> 57.1m as
per September&nbsp;30, 2009 resulted purely from currency translation. There
were no additions or impairments in the first nine months of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>other intangible assets</b>
decreased </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">from EUR 10.3m as per December&nbsp;31, 2008 to</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> EUR 7.8m as per September&nbsp;30,
2009 principally due to depreciation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and
cash equivalents including cash deposits</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased by 58% to
EUR&nbsp;111.1m (EUR 75.1m+ EUR 36.0m) as of September&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2009
compared to EUR&nbsp;70.5m (EUR 67.5m + EUR 3.0m) as of December&nbsp;31, 2008.
The 9M/2009 period end cash position includes, amongst other factors, the
accounting for EUR 6.7m proceeds from the sale of the Aachen office building in
Q1, EUR 2.6m for stock option exercises, the payment of an EUR 8.2m
shareholders&#146; dividend in Q2, comparably higher working capital and lower
capital expenditures, additional EUR 33.0m of bank deposits, and EUR 20.4m of
9M/2009 cumulated net profit.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trade receivables</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased from </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 38.8m</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">as of December&nbsp;31, 2008 to EUR 44.4m as of
September&nbsp;30, 2009 in line with
the increased business volume.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">5. Opportunities and Risks</font></b><a name="a5_OpportunitiesAndRisks_221705"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON believes that the following market trends and <b>opportunities</b> of the relevant end user markets could have a
positive effect on future business:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Short
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Continuing increase of
penetration rates for the production of LED backlighting for LCD-TVs and
Notebooks.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further increased adoption of
LEDs in automotive (e.g. interior lighting, headlights and rear lights).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Early street light orders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mid
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increasing penetration of LED
backlighting in monitors.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Accelerating progress leading
to a broader application of LEDs in general/interior lighting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Emerging e-reader applications
being trialed by newspapers and e-retailers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased emergence of high
volume Silicon Carbide (SiC) production applications and emerging hybrid
automotive and photovoltaic transistor applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of plastic
electronics / flexible organic TFT backplanes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of next generation
NAND and DRAM memory applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased development activity
for non-silicon complex solar cell applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Long
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Progress in research
activities leading to technologies for OLED lighting and organic material large
area deposition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Intensified activity in the
development of new complex semiconductor material applications as substituting
materials in the silicon semiconductor industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of new
applications using Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Carbon
Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is exposed to a series of <b>risks</b>
which are described in detail in chapter 7. &#147;Risk Report&#148; of the Annual Report
2008 and in the section &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in AIXTRON&#146;s 2008 20-F-Report, which has
been filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission on March&nbsp;12,
2009. Copies of the Company&#146;s most recent Annual Report and Form&nbsp;20-F are
available on the Company&#146;s website at http://www.aixtron.com (sections &#147;Investors/Reports&#148;
and &#147;Investors/US-Listing&#148;), as well as on the SEC&#146;s website at
http://www.sec.gov.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April&nbsp;7, 2009, the district court in Aachen
judged in AIXTRON&#146;s favor in the German action for a negative declaratory
judgment against International Rectifier Corporation (&#147;I.R.&#148;), and the German
counterclaim of I.R. was dismissed. This judgement is final.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In February&nbsp;2009, the United States District
Court in California dismissed I.R.&#146;s federal claims against AIXTRON. I.R.
subsequently dropped its federal claims and re-filed its California state law
claims in the California Superior Court for Los Angeles County. I.R. has since
dropped two of its California state law claims against AIXTRON, and is
continuing to assert three of its claims. AIXTRON continues to reject all
allegations involved and continues to defend itself against the allegations and
claims raised in the action.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first nine months of 2009, AIXTRON Management
was not aware of any further significant additions or changes in the risks as
described in the 2008 Annual Report/20-F-Report referred to above.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
