<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">6. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Outlook</font><a name="a6_Outlook_221716"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With a steadily and
strongly increasing order activity after the trough in Q1/2009 (+85% from Q1 to
Q2, +103% from Q2 to Q3), in line with our previous predictions, we remain
positive with respect to the continuation of this increasing LED investment
cycle, which is </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">primarily driven by the
adoption of LED TV applications</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We also remain
confident in our business model and are therefore optimistic about the
increasingly evident medium to long-term trends towards the growing penetration
of LED technologies in a wide range of applications and the consequent positive
effect on future order intake.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
enter the last quarter of the year with a full order book (backlog as per September&nbsp;30:
EUR 152.4m), which has been fuelled by an increasing momentum of LED technology
demand, a rapid return to very high customer production utilization rates, and
improved visibility of LED manufacturers&#146; demand requirements. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Management expects that about EUR 88m of the 9M period end backlog
will be converted into revenues before the end of the year 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
enables us to further increase our revenue guidance for fiscal year 2009 to EUR
280m. We also believe that, due to higher business volume, AIXTRON can deliver
a higher 2009 EBIT margin of 18%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Management will continue to closely watch the USD/EUR exchange rate and the
potential effects on the company&#146;s revenues and profitability.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the last three months of the year, the Company plans to continue to invest in
laboratory equipment and to continue the roll out of the group-wide SAP
Enterprise Software System.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company continually reviews the availability of funds to ensure that the
company has sufficient liquidity to meet the changing needs of the business. In
Management&#146;s opinion, the Company currently has sufficient funds or instruments
in place to ensure that the foreseeable needs of the business can be met.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at September&nbsp;30, 2009, AIXTRON had no binding
agreements for participation financing, company acquisition or transfers of
parts of the Company.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Additional Disclosures<a name="AdditionalDisclosures_001213"></a></font></b></h1>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Accounting Policies</font><a name="a1_AccountingPolicies_001214"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This consolidated
interim financial report of AIXTRON AG has been prepared in accordance with
International Financial Reporting Standards (IFRS) applicable for Interim
Financial Reporting, IAS 34.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It was not audited
according to &#167; 317 HGB or reviewed by a certified auditor.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accounting
policies adopted in this interim financial report are consistent with those
followed in the preparation of the Group&#146;s annual financial statements for the
year ended December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The consolidated interim financial statements
of AIXTRON AG include the following operating subsidiaries (collectively
referred to as &#147;AIXTRON&#148;, &#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148;, or &#147;the Company&#148;): AIXTRON,&nbsp;Inc.,
Sunnyvale, California (USA); AIXTRON Ltd., Cambridge (United Kingdom); AIXTRON
AB, Lund (Sweden); AIXTRON Korea Co. Ltd., Seoul (South Korea); AIXTRON KK,
Tokyo (Japan); and AIXTRON Taiwan Co. Ltd., Hsinchu-City (Taiwan). There were
no significant changes in the consolidated group of companies in comparison
with December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Segment Reporting</font><a name="a2_SegmentReporting_001216"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following segment information has been prepared in
accordance with IFRS 8 &#147;Operating Segments&#148;. As AIXTRON has only one Operating
Segment, the information provided relates only to geographical data.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets
and sells its products in Asia, Europe, and the United States, mainly through
its direct sales organization and cooperation partners.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In presenting
information on the basis of geographical segments, segment revenue is based on
the geographical location of customers. Segment assets are based on the
geographical location of the assets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.
Employees</font></b><a name="a4_Employees_001219"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total number of
employees (*including members of the Executive Board and apprentices) rose from
625 on September&nbsp;30, 2008 to 649 persons on September&nbsp;30, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

were no changes to the composition of the Company&#146;s Executive and Supervisory
Boards as of September&nbsp;30, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON did not conclude or carry out any
material transactions with related parties.</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">7.

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There were no business events with a

position or net assets after September&nbsp;30, 2009, of which the Management
is aware.</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the best of our knowledge, and in accordance with the applicable
reporting principles for interim financial reporting, the interim consolidated
financial statements for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2009 give a
true and fair view of the assets, liabilities, financial position and profit or
loss of the group, and the interim management report of the group includes a
fair review of the development and performance of the business and the position
of the group, together with a description of the principal </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">opportunities and risks associated with the expected development of the
group for the remaining months of the financial year.</font></p>
